<title>妙法蓮華經 (The Lotus Sutra) 觀世音菩薩普門品第二十五 (Chinese)</title>
</head>

The text is based on the electrontic version of <i>Taishō Tripiṭaka</i> 《大正新脩大藏經》available on the Internet [http://21dzk.l.u-tokyo.ac.jp/SAT/](http://21dzk.l.u-tokyo.ac.jp/SAT/) T0262_.09.0056c02 (Kumārajīva's version)maintained by the University of Tokyo.<br><br>

The POS tagging system (with features) is adopted from the [UPenn Chinese POS Tagset](http://www.cis.upenn.edu/~chinese/posguide.3rd.ch.pdf), whilst the dependency system is from the [Stanford Dependencies for Chinese](http://nlp.stanford.edu/software/stanford-dependencies.shtml), with modifications proposed by [John Lee & Y.H. Kong (2012, June)](www.aclweb.org/anthology/N12-1020).<br><br>

Legend:<br>
EMC: Reconstructed Pronunciation of Early Middle Chinese by Pulleyblank (1991)<br>
LMC: Reconstructed Pronunciation of Late Middle Chinese by Pulleyblank (1991)<br>
OM: Reconstructed Pronunciation of Early Mandarin by Pulleyblank (1991)<br>
Pinyin: Pinyin transcription system of modern Chinese by Pulleyblank (1991)<br>
XHZD: 《夏漢字典》Xia-Han zi dian [Tangut-Chinese Dictionary] by 李範文 Li Fanwen (1997).<br><br>

Bibliography:<br>
Lee, J., & Kong, Y. H. (2012, June). A dependency treebank of Classical Chinese poems. In <i>Proceedings of the 2012 Conference of the North American Chapter of the Association for Computational Linguistics: Human Language Technologies</i> (pp. 191-199). Association for Computational Linguistics. [www.aclweb.org/anthology/N12-1020](www.aclweb.org/anthology/N12-1020)<br>
Pulleyblank, E. (1991). <i>Lexicon of reconstructed pronunciation in early Middle Chinese, late Middle Chinese, and early Mandarin.</i> Vancouver [B.C.: UBC Press.<br>
李範文. (1997). 《夏漢字典》 北京 : 中國社會科學出版社.<br>
《大正新脩大藏經》[http://21dzk.l.u-tokyo.ac.jp/SAT/] (http://21dzk.l.u-tokyo.ac.jp/SAT/)<br><br>

Please click [here](https://twwspes.github.io/annodoc/saddharmapundarika_sutram) to read the same chapter in other languages.<br>
